using System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations;
using CafebookModel.Model.ModelWeb.KhachHang;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.RazorPages;

namespace WebCafebookApi.Pages.Account
{
    public class XacMinhOtpViewModel : PageModel
    {
        private readonly IHttpClientFactory _httpClientFactory;
        public XacMinhOtpViewModel(IHttpClientFactory httpClientFactory) => _httpClientFactory = httpClientFactory;

        [BindProperty] public OtpInputModel Input { get; set; } = new();
        public string? ReturnUrl { get; set; }

        [TempData] public string? OtpMessage { get; set; }

        public class OtpInputModel
        {
            public int TempId { get; set; }
            public string TempPassword { get; set; } = string.Empty;
            [Required(ErrorMessage = "Vui lòng nhập mã OTP")] public string OtpCode { get; set; } = string.Empty;
            [Required] public string EditableEmail { get; set; } = string.Empty;
            [Required] public string EditablePhone { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        }

        public IActionResult OnGet(string? returnUrl = null)
        {
            // Bắt buộc phải có TempId từ trang Đăng Ký chuyển qua
            if (TempData["TempId"] == null) return RedirectToPage("/Account/DangKyView");

            ReturnUrl = returnUrl;

            // Lấy dữ liệu đẩy xuống giao diện
            Input.TempId = Convert.ToInt32(TempData["TempId"]);
            Input.TempPassword = TempData["TempPassword"]?.ToString() ?? "";
            Input.EditableEmail = TempData["TempEmail"]?.ToString() ?? "";
            Input.EditablePhone = TempData["TempPhone"]?.ToString() ?? "";

            // Lấy Message để hiển thị, TempData tự Keep nhờ thuộc tính [TempData] ở trên
            OtpMessage = TempData["OtpMessage"]?.ToString();

            return Page();
        }

        public async Task<IActionResult> OnPostAsync(string? returnUrl = null)
        {
            returnUrl ??= Url.Content("~/");
            if (!ModelState.IsValid) return Page();

            var httpClient = _httpClientFactory.CreateClient("ApiClient");
            var apiRequest = new VerifyOtpRequestDto
            {
                TempId = Input.TempId,
                Email = Input.EditableEmail,
                SoDienThoai = Input.EditablePhone,
                Password = Input.TempPassword,
                OtpCode = Input.OtpCode
            };

            var response = await httpClient.PostAsJsonAsync("api/web/khachhang/dangky/verify-otp", apiRequest);
            if (response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
            {
                var apiResponse = await response.Content.ReadFromJsonAsync<DangKyResponseDto>();
                if (apiResponse != null && apiResponse.Success)
                {
                    // XÁC THỰC XONG -> VỀ ĐĂNG NHẬP
                    TempData["ErrorMessage"] = "Xác thực thành công! Tài khoản đã được kích hoạt. Vui lòng đăng nhập.";
                    return RedirectToPage("/Account/DangNhapView", new { returnUrl = returnUrl });
                }
                ModelState.AddModelError(string.Empty, apiResponse?.Message ?? "Mã OTP không đúng hoặc đã hết hạn.");
            }
            return Page();
        }
    }
}

﻿using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.RazorPages;
using Microsoft.Extensions.Caching.Memory;
using System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations;
using System;

namespace WebCafebookApi.Pages.Account // SỬA: Namespace
{
    public class XacNhanMaViewModel : PageModel
    {
        private readonly IMemoryCache _cache;

        public XacNhanMaViewModel(IMemoryCache cache)
        {
            _cache = cache;
        }

        [BindProperty]
        public InputModel Input { get; set; } = new InputModel();

        [TempData]
        public string? ErrorMessage { get; set; }

        public class InputModel
        {
            [Required]
            [HiddenInput]
            public string Email { get; set; } = string.Empty;

            [Required(ErrorMessage = "Vui lòng nhập mã xác nhận.")]
            [Display(Name = "Mã Xác Nhận")]
            [RegularExpression(@"^\d{6}$", ErrorMessage = "Mã xác nhận phải gồm 6 chữ số.")]
            public string VerificationCode { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        }

        public IActionResult OnGet()
        {
            var email = TempData["VerificationEmail"] as string;
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(email))
            {
                return RedirectToPage("./QuenMatKhauView");
            }

            Input.Email = email;
            TempData.Keep("VerificationEmail");
            return Page();
        }

        public IActionResult OnPostAsync()
        {
            if (!ModelState.IsValid)
            {
                return Page();
            }

            string email = Input.Email;
            string cacheKey = $"ForgotPassword_{email}";

            if (_cache.TryGetValue(cacheKey, out string? cachedCode))
            {
                if (cachedCode == Input.VerificationCode)
                {
                    // Mã ĐÚNG. Tạo token reset
                    string resetToken = Guid.NewGuid().ToString("N");
                    string resetCacheKey = $"ResetToken_{email}";
                    var resetCacheOptions = new MemoryCacheEntryOptions()
                        .SetAbsoluteExpiration(TimeSpan.FromMinutes(10));

                    _cache.Set(resetCacheKey, resetToken, resetCacheOptions);
                    _cache.Remove(cacheKey);
                    TempData.Remove("VerificationEmail");

                    return RedirectToPage("./DatLaiMatKhauView", new { email = email, token = resetToken });
                }
                else
                {
                    ErrorMessage = "Mã xác nhận không đúng.";
                    TempData.Keep("VerificationEmail");
                    return Page();
                }
            }
            else
            {
                ErrorMessage = "Mã xác nhận đã hết hạn hoặc không tồn tại.";
                TempData.Keep("VerificationEmail");
                return Page();
            }
        }
    }
}

﻿@page "/nhan-vien/dang-ky-lich"
@model WebCafebookApi.Pages.Employee.DangKyLichViewModel
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "Đăng Ký Lịch Làm Việc";
    Layout = "_Layout_Employee";
}

@section Styles {
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="~/css/DangKyLich.css" asp-append-version="true" />
}

<div class="dkl-container">
    <div class="card shadow-sm border-0 rounded-4">
        
        <div class="card-header bg-white p-4 border-0 pb-0">
            <div class="row align-items-center mb-3">
                <div class="col">
                    <h3 class="fw-bold mb-0 text-dark">Quản Lý Ca Làm Việc</h3>
                    <p class="text-muted small mb-0">Xem nhu cầu và theo dõi ca đã đăng ký</p>
                </div>
            </div>

            <ul class="nav nav-tabs dkl-nav-tabs" id="shiftTabs" role="tablist">
                <li class="nav-item" role="presentation">
                    <button class="nav-link active fw-bold" id="available-tab" data-bs-toggle="tab" data-bs-target="#available-shifts" type="button" role="tab">
                        <span class="material-symbols-outlined align-middle fs-5 me-1">event_available</span> Ca Cần Người
                    </button>
                </li>
                <li class="nav-item" role="presentation">
                    <button class="nav-link fw-bold" id="my-tab" data-bs-toggle="tab" data-bs-target="#my-shifts" type="button" role="tab">
                        <span class="material-symbols-outlined align-middle fs-5 me-1">fact_check</span> Ca Của Tôi
                    </button>
                </li>
            </ul>
        </div>
        
        <div class="card-body p-0">
            <div class="tab-content">
                
                <div class="tab-pane fade show active" id="available-shifts" role="tabpanel">
                    
                    <div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center bg-light p-3 border-bottom">
                        <div class="btn-group shadow-sm" role="group">
                            <input type="radio" class="btn-check" name="vbtn-radio" id="viewList" autocomplete="off" checked>
                            <label class="btn btn-outline-secondary fw-bold" for="viewList"><span class="material-symbols-outlined align-middle">table_rows</span> Danh sách (Ngày)</label>

                            <input type="radio" class="btn-check" name="vbtn-radio" id="viewKanban" autocomplete="off">
                            <label class="btn btn-outline-secondary fw-bold" for="viewKanban"><span class="material-symbols-outlined align-middle">view_kanban</span> Kanban (Tuần)</label>
                        </div>
                        
                        <div class="d-flex gap-2 align-items-center">
                            <button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-secondary rounded-pill fw-bold" id="btnPrev">&lt; Trở lại</button>
                            <input type="date" id="date-filter" class="form-control form-control-sm rounded-pill px-3 shadow-none border-secondary" style="width: 140px;" />
                            <button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-secondary rounded-pill fw-bold" id="btnNext">Tiếp &gt;</button>
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    <div id="mode-list" class="table-responsive">
                        <table class="table table-hover align-middle mb-0">
                            <thead class="bg-white">
                                <tr class="text-muted small text-uppercase">
                                    <th class="ps-4">Ngày Làm</th>
                                    <th>Ca Làm</th>
                                    <th>Số Lượng</th>
                                    <th>Trạng Thái</th>
                                    <th class="text-center pe-4">Thao Tác</th>
                                </tr>
                            </thead>
                            <tbody id="list-body"></tbody>
                        </table>
                    </div>

                    <div id="mode-kanban" class="p-3 bg-light d-none">
                        <div class="dkl-weekly-board" id="kanban-board"></div>
                    </div>
                </div>

                <div class="tab-pane fade" id="my-shifts" role="tabpanel">
                    <div class="table-responsive">
                        <table class="table table-hover align-middle mb-0">
                            <thead class="bg-light">
                                <tr class="text-muted small text-uppercase">
                                    <th class="ps-4">Ngày Làm</th>
                                    <th>Ca Làm</th>
                                    <th>Ghi chú của tôi</th>
                                    <th>Kết Quả</th>
                                    <th class="text-center pe-4">Hủy Đơn</th>
                                </tr>
                            </thead>
                            <tbody id="my-list-body"></tbody>
                        </table>
                    </div>
                </div>

            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
</div>

@section Scripts {
    <script>
        const _apiBaseUrl = "@Model.ApiBaseUrl";
        const _jwtToken = "@Model.JwtToken";
        
        let _config = null;
        let _currentData = [];
        let _currentMode = 'list'; // 'list' | 'kanban'

        const _daysMap = {
            2: "Thứ Hai", 3: "Thứ Ba", 4: "Thứ Tư", 5: "Thứ Năm",
            6: "Thứ Sáu", 7: "Thứ Bảy", 8: "Chủ Nhật"
        };

        function getMonday(d) {
            d = new Date(d);
            var day = d.getDay(), diff = d.getDate() - day + (day === 0 ? -6 : 1);
            return new Date(d.setDate(diff));
        }

        async function init() {
            try {
                const res = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/config`, { headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` } });
                if(res.ok) _config = await res.json();
            } catch(e) { console.error("Lỗi lấy config", e); }

            const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
            $("#date-filter").val(today);
            loadData(today);
        }

        async function loadData(selectedDate) {
            const monday = getMonday(selectedDate);
            const mondayStr = monday.toISOString().split('T')[0];

            $("#list-body, #my-list-body").html('<tr><td colspan="5" class="text-center p-4"><div class="spinner-border text-primary"></div></td></tr>');
            $("#kanban-board").html('<div class="text-center p-4 w-100"><div class="spinner-border text-primary"></div></div>');

            try {
                const response = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/weekly-shifts?monday=${mondayStr}`, { headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` }, cache: 'no-store' });
                if (!response.ok) throw new Error("Lỗi tải dữ liệu");
                _currentData = await response.json();
                
                renderUI();
            } catch (error) {
                Swal.fire('Lỗi', 'Không thể tải dữ liệu.', 'error');
            }
        }

        function renderUI() {
            const selDate = $("#date-filter").val();
            
            // Render Ca Của Tôi (Tất cả trong tuần)
            renderMyShifts(_currentData.filter(x => x.trangThaiCuaToi !== 'Chưa đăng ký'));

            // Lọc & Render Ca Cần Người
            if (_currentMode === 'list') {
                const dayData = _currentData.filter(x => x.trangThaiCuaToi === 'Chưa đăng ký' && x.ngayLam.startsWith(selDate));
                renderList(dayData);
            } else {
                const weekData = _currentData.filter(x => x.trangThaiCuaToi === 'Chưa đăng ký');
                renderKanban(weekData, getMonday(selDate));
            }
        }

        function renderList(data) {
            const $body = $("#list-body").empty();
            if(data.length === 0) return $body.append('<tr><td colspan="5" class="text-center p-5 text-muted">Không có ca trống trong ngày này.</td></tr>');

            data.forEach(s => {
                const dateFormatted = new Date(s.ngayLam).toLocaleDateString('vi-VN', { weekday: 'short', day: '2-digit', month: '2-digit' });
                let statusBadge = '', actionBtn = '';

                if (s.isQuaHan) {
                    statusBadge = '<span class="badge bg-secondary">Đã qua giờ</span>';
                    actionBtn = '<button type="button" class="btn btn-light btn-sm rounded-pill px-3" disabled>Khóa</button>';
                } else if (s.soLuongDaDangKy >= s.soLuongCan) {
                    statusBadge = '<span class="badge bg-danger-subtle text-danger border">Đã đủ người</span>';
                    actionBtn = '<button type="button" class="btn btn-secondary btn-sm rounded-pill px-3" disabled>Đã chốt</button>';
                } else {
                    statusBadge = `<span class="badge bg-light text-dark border">Cần ${s.soLuongCan - s.soLuongDaDangKy} người</span>`;
                    actionBtn = `<button type="button" class="btn btn-primary btn-sm rounded-pill px-3 fw-bold" onclick="registerShift(${s.idNhuCau}, '${s.tenCa}')">Đăng ký</button>`;
                }

                $body.append(`
                    <tr class="${s.isQuaHan ? 'opacity-50' : ''}">
                        <td class="ps-4 fw-bold text-dark">${dateFormatted}</td>
                        <td>
                            <div class="fw-bold text-primary">${s.tenCa}</div>
                            <div class="small text-muted">${s.gioBatDau.substring(0,5)} - ${s.gioKetThuc.substring(0,5)}</div>
                            ${s.ghiChu ? `<div class="small text-info fst-italic mt-1">${s.ghiChu}</div>` : ''}
                        </td>
                        <td><span class="text-muted">${s.soLuongDaDangKy}/${s.soLuongCan}</span></td>
                        <td>${statusBadge}</td>
                        <td class="text-center pe-4">${actionBtn}</td>
                    </tr>
                `);
            });
        }

        function renderKanban(data, monday) {
            const $board = $("#kanban-board").empty();
            if(!_config) return;

            // Chỉ vẽ các cột tương ứng với cấu hình mở cửa (2-8)
            _config.thuMoCua.forEach(dayNum => {
                let offset = dayNum === 8 ? 6 : dayNum - 2; // Chủ nhật là index 6
                let colDate = new Date(monday);
                colDate.setDate(monday.getDate() + offset);
                let dateStr = colDate.toISOString().split('T')[0];
                
                let shiftsForDay = data.filter(d => d.ngayLam.startsWith(dateStr));
                let isToday = (dateStr === new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]);

                let $col = $(`
                    <div class="dkl-column ${isToday ? 'today-col' : ''}">
                        <div class="dkl-col-header">
                            <div class="fw-bold text-uppercase">${_daysMap[dayNum]}</div>
                            <div class="small text-muted">${colDate.toLocaleDateString('vi-VN')}</div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="dkl-col-body"></div>
                    </div>
                `);
                
                let $body = $col.find(".dkl-col-body");

                if(shiftsForDay.length === 0) {
                    $body.append('<div class="text-center text-muted small mt-4 fst-italic">Trống</div>');
                } else {
                    shiftsForDay.forEach(s => {
                        let isFull = s.soLuongDaDangKy >= s.soLuongCan;
                        let cClass = s.isQuaHan ? "card-expired" : (isFull ? "card-full" : "card-available");
                        let sBadge = s.isQuaHan ? `<span class="badge bg-secondary w-100">Qua giờ</span>` : (isFull ? `<span class="badge bg-danger w-100">Đã đủ</span>` : `<span class="badge bg-light text-dark border w-100">Cần ${s.soLuongCan - s.soLuongDaDangKy}</span>`);
                        let aBtn = (s.isQuaHan || isFull) ? '' : `<button type="button" class="btn btn-primary btn-sm w-100 mt-2 fw-bold" onclick="registerShift(${s.idNhuCau}, '${s.tenCa}')">Đăng ký</button>`;

                        $body.append(`
                            <div class="dkl-card ${cClass}">
                                <div class="fw-bold text-primary mb-1">${s.tenCa}</div>
                                <div class="small text-muted mb-2 fw-medium">
                                    <span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-6 align-middle">schedule</span> ${s.gioBatDau.substring(0,5)} - ${s.gioKetThuc.substring(0,5)}
                                </div>
                                ${sBadge}
                                ${aBtn}
                            </div>
                        `);
                    });
                }
                $board.append($col);
            });
        }

        function renderMyShifts(data) {
            const $body = $("#my-list-body").empty();
            if(data.length === 0) return $body.append('<tr><td colspan="5" class="text-center p-5 text-muted">Bạn chưa đăng ký ca nào.</td></tr>');

            data.forEach(s => {
                const dateFormatted = new Date(s.ngayLam).toLocaleDateString('vi-VN', { weekday: 'short', day: '2-digit', month: '2-digit' });
                let badge = s.trangThaiCuaToi === 'Chờ duyệt'
                    ? '<span class="badge bg-warning-subtle text-warning border border-warning-subtle"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-6 align-middle">hourglass_empty</span> Chờ quản lý duyệt</span>'
                    : '<span class="badge bg-success-subtle text-success border border-success-subtle"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-6 align-middle">check_circle</span> Lịch chính thức</span>';
                
                let actionBtn = s.trangThaiCuaToi === 'Chờ duyệt'
                    ? `<button type="button" class="btn btn-outline-danger btn-sm rounded-pill px-3" onclick="cancelShift(${s.idLichCuaToi})">Hủy ca</button>`
                    : '<span class="text-muted small fst-italic">Không thể hủy</span>';

                $body.append(`
                    <tr>
                        <td class="ps-4 fw-bold text-dark">${dateFormatted}</td>
                        <td>
                            <div class="fw-bold text-primary">${s.tenCa}</div>
                            <div class="small text-muted">${s.gioBatDau.substring(0,5)} - ${s.gioKetThuc.substring(0,5)}</div>
                        </td>
                        <td>${s.ghiChuCuaToi ? `<span class="badge bg-light text-dark text-wrap text-start border p-2"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-6 align-middle text-primary">push_pin</span> ${s.ghiChuCuaToi}</span>` : '<span class="text-muted small">--</span>'}</td>
                        <td>${badge}</td>
                        <td class="text-center pe-4">${actionBtn}</td>
                    </tr>
                `);
            });
        }

        async function registerShift(idNhuCau, tenCa) {
            const { value: note } = await Swal.fire({
                title: `Đăng ký ${tenCa}`,
                input: 'text',
                inputLabel: 'Bạn muốn đăng ký vị trí nào? (VD: Thu ngân, Phục vụ tầng 2...)',
                inputPlaceholder: 'Ghi chú cho quản lý...',
                showCancelButton: true,
                confirmButtonText: 'Xác nhận',
                cancelButtonText: 'Đóng',
                confirmButtonColor: '#6F4E37'
            });

            if (note !== undefined) {
                try {
                    const response = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/register`, {
                        method: 'POST',
                        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` },
                        body: JSON.stringify({ idNhuCau, ghiChuNhanVien: note })
                    });

                    if (response.ok) {
                        Swal.fire({ title: 'Thành công', text: 'Yêu cầu đã được gửi.', icon: 'success', timer: 1500, showConfirmButton: false });
                        loadData($("#date-filter").val());
                        var tab = new bootstrap.Tab(document.querySelector('#my-tab'));
                        tab.show();
                    } else {
                        let msg = "Lỗi."; try { const err = await response.json(); msg = err.message || msg; } catch(e) {}
                        Swal.fire('Không thể đăng ký', msg, 'warning');
                    }
                } catch (error) { Swal.fire('Lỗi', 'Mất kết nối máy chủ', 'error'); }
            }
        }

        async function cancelShift(idLich) {
            if ((await Swal.fire({title: 'Hủy đăng ký?', text: "Rút lại yêu cầu này?", icon: 'warning', showCancelButton: true, confirmButtonColor: '#D32F2F', confirmButtonText: 'Hủy'})).isConfirmed) {
                const response = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/cancel/${idLich}`, { method: 'DELETE', headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` } });
                if (response.ok) {
                    Swal.fire({ title: 'Đã hủy', icon: 'success', timer: 1000, showConfirmButton: false });
                    loadData($("#date-filter").val());
                } else {
                    let msg = "Lỗi."; try { const err = await response.json(); msg = err.message || msg; } catch(e) {}
                    Swal.fire('Lỗi', msg, 'error');
                }
            }
        }

        $(document).ready(function() {
            // Chuyển Mode List / Kanban
            $("input[name='vbtn-radio']").change(function() {
                _currentMode = this.id === 'viewKanban' ? 'kanban' : 'list';
                if(_currentMode === 'kanban') { $("#mode-list").addClass("d-none"); $("#mode-kanban").removeClass("d-none"); }
                else { $("#mode-kanban").addClass("d-none"); $("#mode-list").removeClass("d-none"); }
                renderUI();
            });

            // Thay đổi Ngày/Tuần
            $("#date-filter").on("change", function() { loadData($(this).val()); });
            
            $("#btnPrev").click(function() {
                let d = new Date($("#date-filter").val());
                d.setDate(d.getDate() - (_currentMode === 'list' ? 1 : 7));
                $("#date-filter").val(d.toISOString().split('T')[0]).trigger('change');
            });
            
            $("#btnNext").click(function() {
                let d = new Date($("#date-filter").val());
                d.setDate(d.getDate() + (_currentMode === 'list' ? 1 : 7));
                $("#date-filter").val(d.toISOString().split('T')[0]).trigger('change');
            });

            init();
        });
    </script>
}

using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.RazorPages;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authorization;

namespace WebCafebookApi.Pages.Employee
{
    [Authorize]
    public class DangKyLichViewModel : PageModel
    {
        private readonly IHttpClientFactory _httpClientFactory;
        public string ApiBaseUrl { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string? JwtToken { get; set; }

        public DangKyLichViewModel(IHttpClientFactory httpClientFactory)
        {
            _httpClientFactory = httpClientFactory;
        }

        public void OnGet()
        {
            JwtToken = HttpContext.Session.GetString("JwtToken");
            var client = _httpClientFactory.CreateClient("ApiClient");
            ApiBaseUrl = $"{client.BaseAddress}api/web/nhanvien/dangkylichweb";
        }
    }
}

        $(document).ready(function () {
        var errorMsg = '@Html.Raw(Model.ErrorMessage?.Replace("'", "\\'"))';
        if (errorMsg && errorMsg.trim() !== '') {
        Swal.fire({
        icon: 'error',

        confirmButtonColor: '#D32F2F',
        confirmButtonText: 'Thử lại'
        });
        }

        $('#employeeLoginForm').on('submit', function (e) {
        if ($(this).valid()) {
        var btn = $('#btnLogin');
        btn.prop('disabled', true);
        btn.find('.btn-text').text('ĐANG XỬ LÝ...');
        $('#loginSpinner').removeClass('d-none');
        }

        });

using System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations;
using System.Security.Claims;
using CafebookModel.Model.Shared;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authentication;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authentication.Cookies;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.RazorPages;
using System.Text.Json;

namespace WebCafebookApi.Pages.Employee
{
    [IgnoreAntiforgeryToken]
    public class DangNhapEmployeeModel : PageModel
    {
        private readonly IHttpClientFactory _httpClientFactory;
        public DangNhapEmployeeModel(IHttpClientFactory httpClientFactory)
        {
            _httpClientFactory = httpClientFactory;
        }

        [BindProperty]
        public InputModel Input { get; set; } = new();

        [TempData]
        public string? ErrorMessage { get; set; }

        public string? ReturnUrl { get; set; }

        public class InputModel
        {
            [Required(ErrorMessage = "Vui lòng nhập Tên đăng nhập, Email hoặc SĐT")]
            public string TenDangNhap { get; set; } = string.Empty;

            [Required(ErrorMessage = "Vui lòng nhập mật khẩu")]
            [DataType(DataType.Password)]
            public string MatKhau { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        }

        public async Task OnGetAsync(string? returnUrl = null)
        {
            await HttpContext.SignOutAsync(CookieAuthenticationDefaults.AuthenticationScheme);
            HttpContext.Session.Remove("JwtToken");
            HttpContext.Session.Remove("AvatarUrl");

            ReturnUrl = returnUrl ?? Url.Content("~/Employee/TongQuanView");
        }

        public async Task<IActionResult> OnPostAsync(string? returnUrl = null)
        {
            if (!ModelState.IsValid)
            {
                return Page();
            }

            try
            {
                var httpClient = _httpClientFactory.CreateClient("ApiClient");
                var apiRequest = new LoginRequest
                {
                    Username = Input.TenDangNhap,
                    Password = Input.MatKhau
                };

                var response = await httpClient.PostAsJsonAsync("api/shared/Auth/login-nhan-vien", apiRequest);

                if (response.IsSuccessStatusCode)
                {
                    var apiResponse = await response.Content.ReadFromJsonAsync<LoginResponse>();

                    if (apiResponse != null && !string.IsNullOrEmpty(apiResponse.Token))
                    {
                        var claims = new List<Claim>
                        {
                            new Claim(ClaimTypes.NameIdentifier, apiResponse.IdNhanVien.ToString()),
                            new Claim(ClaimTypes.Name, apiResponse.HoTen),
                            new Claim(ClaimTypes.Role, apiResponse.TenVaiTro)
                        };

                        if (apiResponse.Quyen != null)
                        {
                            foreach (var quyen in apiResponse.Quyen)
                            {
                                claims.Add(new Claim("Permission", quyen));
                            }
                        }

                        var claimsIdentity = new ClaimsIdentity(claims, CookieAuthenticationDefaults.AuthenticationScheme);
                        var authProperties = new AuthenticationProperties
                        {
                            ExpiresUtc = DateTimeOffset.UtcNow.AddHours(8),
                            IsPersistent = true
                        };

                        await HttpContext.SignInAsync(CookieAuthenticationDefaults.AuthenticationScheme, new ClaimsPrincipal(claimsIdentity), authProperties);

                        string avatar = apiResponse.AnhDaiDien ?? "";
                        if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(avatar) && !avatar.StartsWith("http"))
                        {
                            var apiBaseUrl = httpClient.BaseAddress?.ToString().TrimEnd('/');
                            if (!avatar.StartsWith("/")) avatar = "/" + avatar;
                            avatar = $"{apiBaseUrl}{avatar}"; 
                        }

                        HttpContext.Session.SetString("JwtToken", apiResponse.Token);
                        HttpContext.Session.SetString("AvatarUrl", avatar);

                        if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(returnUrl) || returnUrl == "/")
                        {
                            return RedirectToPage("/Employee/TongQuanView");
                        }

                        return LocalRedirect(returnUrl);
                    }
                }
                else
                {
                    var errorContent = await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync();
                    try
                    {
                        var errorJson = JsonSerializer.Deserialize<JsonElement>(errorContent);
                        if (errorJson.TryGetProperty("message", out var msg))
                        {
                            ErrorMessage = msg.GetString();
                            return Page();
                        }
                    }
                    catch { }
                }

                ErrorMessage = "Tài khoản hoặc mật khẩu không chính xác.";
                return Page();
            }
            catch (Exception)
            {
                ErrorMessage = "Không thể kết nối đến máy chủ. Vui lòng thử lại sau.";
                return Page();
            }
        }
    }
}

@section Scripts {
    <script>
        const _apiBaseUrl = "@Model.ApiBaseUrl";
        const _jwtToken = "@Model.JwtToken";

        // Thiết lập giá trị min cho input date là ngày hôm nay
        const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
        document.getElementById("txtTuNgay").setAttribute("min", today);
        document.getElementById("txtDenNgay").setAttribute("min", today);

        // Ràng buộc Từ ngày <= Đến ngày
        $("#txtTuNgay").on("change", function() {
            $("#txtDenNgay").setAttribute("min", this.value);
        });

        // Load Lịch sử
        async function loadHistory() {
            $("#history-container").html('<div class="text-center p-4"><div class="spinner-border text-primary"></div></div>');
            try {
                const res = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/history`, {
                    headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` }
                });
                if (!res.ok) throw new Error("Lỗi tải dữ liệu");
                const data = await res.json();
                renderHistory(data);
            } catch (err) {
                $("#history-container").html(`<div class="alert alert-danger m-3">${err.message}</div>`);
            }
        }

        function renderHistory(list) {
            const $cont = $("#history-container").empty();
            if (list.length === 0) {
                $cont.html('<div class="text-center text-muted p-5"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-1 text-light">inbox</span><br/>Bạn chưa có đơn xin nghỉ nào.</div>');
                return;
            }

            list.forEach(item => {
                let badgeClass = "bg-warning text-dark"; // Chờ duyệt
                if (item.trangThai === "Đã duyệt") badgeClass = "bg-success text-white";
                if (item.trangThai === "Đã từ chối") badgeClass = "bg-danger text-white";

                const formatDate = (dateStr) => {
                    const d = new Date(dateStr);
                    return d.toLocaleDateString('vi-VN');
                };

                const ghiChuHtml = item.ghiChuPheDuyet
                    ? `<div class="mt-2 pt-2 border-top small"><span class="fw-bold text-dark">Phản hồi từ ${item.nguoiDuyet}:</span> <span class="text-primary fst-italic">${item.ghiChuPheDuyet}</span></div>`
                    : '';

                $cont.append(`
                    <div class="dxn-history-item mb-3">
                        <div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-start mb-2">
                            <h6 class="fw-bold m-0" style="color: #4E342E;">${item.loaiDon}</h6>
                            <span class="badge ${badgeClass} rounded-pill px-3 py-1">${item.trangThai}</span>
                        </div>
                        <div class="text-muted small mb-2 d-flex align-items-center">
                            <span class="material-symbols-outlined me-1" style="font-size: 16px;">calendar_month</span>
                            ${formatDate(item.ngayBatDau)} &rarr; ${formatDate(item.ngayKetThuc)}
                        </div>
                        <div class="small" style="color: #616161;">
                            <span class="fw-bold">Lý do:</span> ${item.lyDo}
                        </div>
                        ${ghiChuHtml}
                    </div>
                `);
            });
        }

        // Submit Đơn
        $("#formTaoDon").submit(async function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();

            const tuNgay = $("#txtTuNgay").val();
            const denNgay = $("#txtDenNgay").val();

            if(tuNgay > denNgay) {
                Swal.fire("Lỗi", "Ngày kết thúc phải lớn hơn hoặc bằng ngày bắt đầu.", "error");
                return;
            }

            const payload = {
                loaiDon: $("#cboLoaiDon").val(),
                lyDo: $("#txtLyDo").val().trim(),
                ngayBatDau: tuNgay,
                ngayKetThuc: denNgay
            };

            const btn = $("#btnSubmitDon");
            btn.prop("disabled", true).html('<div class="spinner-border spinner-border-sm me-2"></div> Đang gửi...');

            try {
                const res = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/create`, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` },
                    body: JSON.stringify(payload)
                });
                
                const data = await res.json();
                if (!res.ok) throw new Error(data.message || "Đã xảy ra lỗi");

                Swal.fire("Thành công", data.message, "success");
                $("#formTaoDon")[0].reset();
                loadHistory();
            } catch (err) {
                Swal.fire("Lỗi Gửi Đơn", err.message, "error");
            } finally {
                btn.prop("disabled", false).html('<span class="material-symbols-outlined me-2">send</span> Gửi Đơn Xin Nghỉ');
            }
        });

        $(document).ready(() => {
            loadHistory();
            $("#btnRefresh").click(loadHistory);
        });
    </script>
}

using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authorization;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.RazorPages;

namespace WebCafebookApi.Pages.Employee
{
    [Authorize]
    public class DonXinNghiViewModel : PageModel
    {
        private readonly IHttpClientFactory _httpClientFactory;

        public string ApiBaseUrl { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string? JwtToken { get; set; }

        public DonXinNghiViewModel(IHttpClientFactory httpClientFactory)
        {
            _httpClientFactory = httpClientFactory;
        }

        public IActionResult OnGet()
        {
            JwtToken = HttpContext.Session.GetString("JwtToken");
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(JwtToken)) return RedirectToPage("/Employee/DangNhapEmployee");

            var client = _httpClientFactory.CreateClient("ApiClient");
            ApiBaseUrl = $"{client.BaseAddress}api/web/nhanvien/donxinnghiweb";

            return Page();
        }
    }
}

@section Scripts {
    <script>
        const _idHoaDon = @Model.IdHoaDon;
        const _apiBaseUrl = "@Model.ApiBaseUrl";
        const _jwtToken = "@Model.JwtToken";
        const _defaultImage = "@HinhAnhPaths.WebDefaultFoodIcon";

        let _allSanPhams = [];
        let _chiTietItems = {};
        let _currentPromoId = 0; 
        let _currentPromoName = ""; 
        
        const formatCurrency = (number) => new Intl.NumberFormat('vi-VN', { style: 'currency', currency: 'VND' }).format(number);

        async function callApi(endpoint, method, data) {
            try {
                const res = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/${endpoint}`, {
                    method: method, headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` },
                    body: data ? JSON.stringify(data) : null
                });
                if (!res.ok) throw new Error(await res.text());
                const contentType = res.headers.get("content-type");
                return contentType && contentType.includes("json") ? await res.json() : await res.text();
            } catch (err) {
                Swal.fire('Lỗi Thao Tác', err.message, 'error');
                return null;
            }
        }

        async function loadData() {
            const data = await callApi(`load/${_idHoaDon}`, 'GET');
            if(data) {
                _allSanPhams = data.sanPhams;
                data.chiTietItems.forEach(item => _chiTietItems[item.idChiTietHoaDon] = item);
                
                // Render Categories
                data.danhMucs.forEach(dm => $("#category-list").append(`<li class="nav-item"><a class="nav-link" href="#" data-id="${dm.idDanhMuc}"><span class="material-symbols-outlined">label</span> ${dm.tenLoaiSP}</a></li>`));
                
                // Render Promos
                data.khuyenMais.forEach(km => $("#cboKhuyenMai").append(`<option value="${km.idKhuyenMai}">${km.tenKhuyenMai}</option>`));
                
                renderProducts(_allSanPhams);
                renderBill(data.hoaDonInfo);
            }
        }

        function renderProducts(list) {
            const $list = $("#product-list").empty();
            if(!list.length) return $list.html('<p class="text-center text-muted p-4 w-100">Không có sản phẩm</p>');
            list.forEach(sp => {
                $list.append(`
                    <div class="gmw-product-card" data-id="${sp.idSanPham}">
                        <img src="${sp.hinhAnh}" onerror="this.onerror=null; this.src='${_defaultImage}';">
                        <div class="p-2 text-center">
                            <div class="gmw-product-name text-truncate fw-bold">${sp.tenSanPham}</div>
                            <div class="gmw-product-price text-danger fw-bold">${formatCurrency(sp.donGia)}</div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                `);
                $list.children().last().data('sanpham', sp);
            });
        }

        function renderBill(info) {
                    $("#lblTieuDeHoaDon").text(`Hóa đơn - ${info.soBan}`);
                    $("#lblTongTien").text(formatCurrency(info.tongTienGoc));
                    $("#lblTienGiam").text(formatCurrency(info.giamGia));
                    $("#lblThanhTien").text(formatCurrency(info.thanhTien));
            
                    _currentPromoId = info.idKhuyenMai || 0;
                    if(_currentPromoId === 0) {
                        $("#lblTenKhuyenMaiDangDung").text("");
                        $("#btnMoPopupKhuyenMai").text("Chọn Mã").removeClass("btn-success").addClass("btn-outline-primary");
                    }

                    const $body = $("#bill-details-body").empty();
                    const items = Object.values(_chiTietItems).sort((a, b) => a.idChiTietHoaDon - b.idChiTietHoaDon);
            
                    if(!items.length) return $body.html('<tr><td colspan="3" class="text-center text-muted py-4">Chưa có món</td></tr>');
            
                    items.forEach(item => {
                        $body.append(`
                            <tr>
                                <td>
                                    <div class="fw-bold">${item.tenSanPham}</div>
                                    <div class="text-muted small">${formatCurrency(item.donGia)} ${item.ghiChu ? `<br/><i class="text-primary">${item.ghiChu}</i>` : ''}</div>
                                </td>
                                <td>
                                    <div class="d-flex align-items-center justify-content-center gap-2">
                                        <button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-danger px-2 py-0 fs-5 btn-giam" data-id="${item.idChiTietHoaDon}">-</button>
                                        <span class="fw-bold">${item.soLuong}</span>
                                        <button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-success px-2 py-0 fs-5 btn-tang" data-id="${item.idChiTietHoaDon}">+</button>
                                    </div>
                                </td>
                                <td class="text-center">
                                    <button class="btn btn-sm text-danger btn-xoa" data-id="${item.idChiTietHoaDon}"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-5">delete</span></button>
                                </td>
                            </tr>
                        `);
                    });
                }

        $(document).ready(function() {
            loadData();

            // Filter UI
            $("#category-list").on("click", ".nav-link", function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                $("#category-list .nav-link").removeClass("active"); $(this).addClass("active");
                const catId = $(this).data("id");
                const kw = $("#search-bar").val().toLowerCase();
                let filtered = catId ? _allSanPhams.filter(s => s.idDanhMuc == catId) : _allSanPhams;
                if(kw) filtered = filtered.filter(s => s.tenSanPham.toLowerCase().includes(kw));
                renderProducts(filtered);
            });

            $("#search-bar").on("keyup", () => $("#category-list .active").click());

            // Add Product
            $("#product-list").on("click", ".gmw-product-card", async function() {
                const sp = $(this).data('sanpham');
                const { value: note } = await Swal.fire({ title: `Thêm ${sp.tenSanPham}`, input: 'text', inputPlaceholder: 'Ghi chú (không bắt buộc)', showCancelButton: true, confirmButtonColor: '#6F4E37', confirmButtonText: 'Thêm' });
                if(note !== undefined) {
                    const res = await callApi('add-item', 'POST', { idHoaDon: _idHoaDon, idSanPham: sp.idSanPham, soLuong: 1, ghiChu: note.trim() });
                    if(res) { _chiTietItems[res.newItem.idChiTietHoaDon] = res.newItem; renderBill(res.updatedHoaDonInfo); }
                }
            });

            // Adjust Quantity
            const changeQty = async (id, delta) => {
                const item = _chiTietItems[id];
                const res = await callApi('update-quantity', 'PUT', { idChiTietHoaDon: id, soLuongMoi: item.soLuong + delta });
                if(res) {
                    if(item.soLuong + delta <= 0) delete _chiTietItems[id];
                    else item.soLuong += delta;
                    renderBill(res);
                }
            };
            $("#bill-details-body").on("click", ".btn-tang", function() { changeQty($(this).data("id"), 1); });
            $("#bill-details-body").on("click", ".btn-giam", function() { changeQty($(this).data("id"), -1); });
            
            // Delete Item
            $("#bill-details-body").on("click", ".btn-xoa", async function() {
                const id = $(this).data("id");
                if((await Swal.fire({title:'Xóa món?', icon:'warning', showCancelButton:true, confirmButtonColor:'#d33'})).isConfirmed){
                    const res = await callApi(`delete-item/${id}`, 'DELETE');
                    if(res) { delete _chiTietItems[id]; renderBill(res); }
                }
            });

            // Send to Kitchen
            $("#btnGuiBep").click(async function() {
                const res = await callApi(`send-to-kitchen/${_idHoaDon}`, 'POST');
                if(res) Swal.fire('Thành công', 'Đã báo bếp thành công!', 'success');
            });
        });
        $('#modalKhuyenMai').on('show.bs.modal', async function () {
                    const $container = $("#promo-list-container");
                    $container.html('<div class="text-center p-4"><div class="spinner-border text-primary"></div><p class="mt-2 text-muted">Đang tìm mã giảm giá...</p></div>');
            
                    const promos = await callApi(`khuyenmai-available/${_idHoaDon}`, 'GET');
                    if(promos) {
                        $container.empty();
                        if(promos.length === 0) {
                            $container.html('<div class="text-center text-muted p-4">Không có mã khuyến mãi nào.</div>');
                            return;
                        }

                        promos.forEach(km => {
                            const isDis = km.isEligible ? "" : "disabled";
                            const reasonHtml = km.isEligible ? `<div class="gmw-promo-discount">- ${formatCurrency(km.calculatedDiscount)}</div>` : `<div class="gmw-promo-reason"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-6 align-middle">error</span> ${km.ineligibilityReason}</div>`;
                            const activeBadge = (_currentPromoId === km.idKhuyenMai) ? '<div class="gmw-promo-active-badge">Đang dùng</div>' : '';

                            $container.append(`
                                <div class="gmw-promo-card ${isDis}" data-id="${km.idKhuyenMai}" data-eligible="${km.isEligible}" data-name="${km.tenChuongTrinh}">
                                    ${activeBadge}
                                    <div class="gmw-promo-title">${km.maKhuyenMai} - ${km.tenChuongTrinh}</div>
                                    <div class="gmw-promo-desc mb-2">${km.dieuKienApDung}</div>
                                    ${reasonHtml}
                                </div>
                            `);
                        });
                    }
                });

                // Click chọn 1 Khuyến Mãi trong Popup
                $("#promo-list-container").on("click", ".gmw-promo-card", async function() {
                    if($(this).data("eligible") === false) return; // Bỏ qua nếu ko đủ điều kiện

                    const idKM = $(this).data("id");
                    _currentPromoName = $(this).data("name");

                    const res = await callApi('apply-promotion', 'PUT', { idHoaDon: _idHoaDon, idKhuyenMai: idKM });
                    if(res) {
                        $('#modalKhuyenMai').modal('hide');
                        $("#lblTenKhuyenMaiDangDung").text(`Mã: ${_currentPromoName}`);
                        $("#btnMoPopupKhuyenMai").text("Đổi Mã").removeClass("btn-outline-primary").addClass("btn-success");
                        renderBill(res);
                        Swal.fire({ title: 'Áp dụng mã thành công!', icon: 'success', toast: true, position: 'top-end', showConfirmButton: false, timer: 2000 });
                    }
                });

                // Nút Bỏ chọn Khuyến mãi
                $("#btnBoChonKhuyenMai").click(async function() {
                    if(_currentPromoId === 0) return $('#modalKhuyenMai').modal('hide');

                    const res = await callApi('apply-promotion', 'PUT', { idHoaDon: _idHoaDon, idKhuyenMai: 0 });
                    if(res) {
                        $('#modalKhuyenMai').modal('hide');
                        _currentPromoName = "";
                        renderBill(res);
                        Swal.fire({ title: 'Đã hủy mã giảm giá!', icon: 'info', toast: true, position: 'top-end', showConfirmButton: false, timer: 2000 });
                    }
                });

    </script>
}

using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.RazorPages;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authorization;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.DataProtection; 

namespace WebCafebookApi.Pages.Employee
{
    [Authorize]
    public class GoiMonViewModel : PageModel
    {
        private readonly IHttpClientFactory _httpClientFactory;
        private readonly IDataProtector _protector; 

        public int IdHoaDon { get; set; }
        public string ApiBaseUrl { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string? JwtToken { get; set; }

        [TempData]
        public string? ErrorMessage { get; set; }

        public GoiMonViewModel(IHttpClientFactory httpClientFactory, IDataProtectionProvider provider)
        {
            _httpClientFactory = httpClientFactory;
            _protector = provider.CreateProtector("Cafebook.HoaDon.Security");
        }

        public IActionResult OnGet(string? maHoaDon)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(maHoaDon))
            {
                TempData["ErrorMessage"] = "Không tìm thấy thông tin Hóa đơn.";
                return RedirectToPage("/Employee/SoDoBanView");
            }

            try
            {
                string rawId = _protector.Unprotect(maHoaDon);
                IdHoaDon = int.Parse(rawId);
            }
            catch (Exception)
            {
                ErrorMessage = "Mã đường dẫn không hợp lệ hoặc đã bị can thiệp!";
                return Page();
            }

            JwtToken = HttpContext.Session.GetString("JwtToken");
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(JwtToken)) return RedirectToPage("/Employee/DangNhapEmployee");

            var client = _httpClientFactory.CreateClient("ApiClient");
            ApiBaseUrl = $"{client.BaseAddress}api/web/nhanvien/goimonweb";

            return Page();
        }
    }
}

﻿@page "/nhan-vien/ho-tro-khach-hang/"
@model WebCafebookApi.Pages.Employee.HoTroKhachHangViewModel
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "Trung tâm Hỗ trợ Khách hàng";

@section Styles {

<div class="htnv-dashboard-grid">
    @* CỘT 1: DANH SÁCH PHIẾU *@
    <div class="htnv-ticket-list-wrapper">
        <div class="htnv-header-box">

            </div>

        <form method="post" id="chatForm" class="htnv-chat-form" asp-antiforgery="true">

                <input id="chatMessageInput" class="htnv-chat-input" placeholder="Nhân viên nhập phản hồi..." autocomplete="off" disabled />

@section Scripts {
    <partial name="_ValidationScriptsPartial" />
    <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/microsoft-signalr/8.0.0/signalr.min.js"></script>
    <script>
        const apiBaseUrl = '@Model.ApiBaseUrl'.replace(/\/$/, "");
        $(document).ready(function () {
        const $ticketListContainer = $('#ticket-list-container');
        const $chatHistory = $('#chat-history');
        const $summaryCardContent = $('#summary-card-content');
        const $chatForm = $('#chatForm');
        const $chatInput = $('#chatMessageInput');
        const $sendButton = $('#sendButton');
        const $resolveButton = $('#resolveButton');
            
        const jwtToken = $('#JwtToken').val() || null;
        const antiForgeryToken = $('input[name="__RequestVerificationToken"]').val();

        let currentTicketId = null;
        let currentGroupName = null;
        let currentTicketData = null;

        const headers = { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'RequestVerificationToken': antiForgeryToken };
        if (jwtToken) headers['Authorization'] = 'Bearer ' + jwtToken;

        // 1. Hàm vẽ 1 tin nhắn duy nhất (Dùng cho cả Load và Realtime) [cite: 23, 24]
        function appendSingleMessage(msg) {
        const isUser = msg.loaiTinNhan === 'KhachHang';
        const isStaff = msg.loaiTinNhan === 'NhanVien';
        const rowClass = isUser ? 'htnv-user-row' : (isStaff ? 'htnv-staff-row' : 'htnv-bot-row');
        const avatarClass = isUser ? 'htnv-avatar-user' : (isStaff ? 'htnv-avatar-staff' : 'htnv-avatar-bot');
        const avatarIcon = isUser ? 'person' : (isStaff ? 'support_agent' : 'smart_toy');
        const bubbleClass = isUser ? 'htnv-bubble-user' : (isStaff ? 'htnv-bubble-staff' : 'htnv-bubble-bot');
                
        let cleanText = (msg.noiDung || '').replace(/\[BUTTON:\s*(.*?)\s*\|\s*(.*?)\]/g, "");
        cleanText = cleanText.replace(/\n/g, '<br />').replace(/\*\*(.*?)\*\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>');
        const time = new Date(msg.thoiGian).toLocaleTimeString('vi-VN', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' });
                
        const html = `
        <div class="htnv-message-row ${rowClass}">
        <div class="htnv-avatar ${avatarClass}"><span class="material-symbols-outlined">${avatarIcon}</span></div>
        <div class="htnv-msg-content">
        <div class="htnv-bubble ${bubbleClass}">${cleanText}</div>
        <div class="htnv-bubble-time ${isUser ? 'text-end' : 'text-start'}">${time}</div>
        </div>
        </div>`;
                
        $chatHistory.append(html);
        $chatHistory.scrollTop($chatHistory[0].scrollHeight); // Cuộn xuống cuối [cite: 25]
        }

        // 2. Load danh sách phiếu hỗ trợ
        async function loadTicketList() {
        try {
        const response = await fetch(`${apiBaseUrl}/api/web/nhanvien/hotro/tickets`, { method: 'GET', headers: headers });
        if (!response.ok) throw new Error('Failed to load');
        const tickets = await response.json();
                    
        if (tickets.length === 0) {
        $ticketListContainer.html('<div class="htnv-empty-state p-3">Không có yêu cầu hỗ trợ nào.</div>');
        return;
        }
        $ticketListContainer.empty();
        tickets.forEach(ticket => {
        const time = new Date(ticket.thoiGianTao).toLocaleString('vi-VN');
        const isPending = ticket.trangThai === 'Chờ xử lý';
        const statusClass = isPending ? 'htnv-status-pending' : '';
        const indicatorHtml = isPending ? '<span class="htnv-status-indicator"></span>' : '';
        const statusColor = isPending ? 'text-danger' : 'text-success';
                        
        const ticketHtml = `
        <div class="htnv-ticket-item ${statusClass}" data-id="${ticket.idThongBao}">
        <div class="d-flex justify-content-between">
        <strong>${ticket.tenKhachHang}</strong>
        <span class="htnv-ticket-time ${statusColor}">${ticket.trangThai}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="htnv-ticket-preview">${ticket.noiDungYeuCau || '...'}</div>
        <small>${time}</small>
        ${indicatorHtml}
        </div>`;
        $ticketListContainer.append(ticketHtml);
        });
        } catch (error) {
        $ticketListContainer.html('<div class="htnv-empty-state p-3">Lỗi tải danh sách.</div>');
        }
        }

        // 3. Load chi tiết và Join phòng chat
        async function loadTicketDetail(id) {
        if (!id) return;
        currentTicketId = id;
        $('.htnv-ticket-item').removeClass('active');
        $(`.htnv-ticket-item[data-id="${id}"]`).addClass('active');

        $chatInput.prop('disabled', true); $sendButton.prop('disabled', true);
                
        try {
        const response = await fetch(`${apiBaseUrl}/api/web/nhanvien/hotro/ticket/${id}`, { method: 'GET', headers: headers });
        const ticketData = await response.json();
        currentTicketData = ticketData;
                    
        $chatHistory.empty();
        if (ticketData.lichSuChat && ticketData.lichSuChat.length > 0) {
        ticketData.lichSuChat.forEach(msg => appendSingleMessage(msg));
        } else {
        $chatHistory.html('<div class="htnv-empty-state">Chưa có tin nhắn</div>');
        }

        $summaryCardContent.html(`
        <p><strong>Khách hàng:</strong> <span>${ticketData.tenKhachHang}</span></p>
        <p><strong>Phiếu:</strong> <span>#${ticketData.idThongBao}</span></p>
        <p><strong>Trạng thái:</strong> <span class="badge bg-warning text-dark fs-6" id="chatHeaderStatus">${ticketData.trangThai}</span></p>
        <hr />
        <p><strong>Yêu cầu ban đầu:</strong> <div class="htnv-request-content">${ticketData.noiDungYeuCau || ''}</div></p>
        <p><strong>Ghi chú hệ thống:</strong> <div class="htnv-request-content" style="border: 1px dashed var(--cf-terracotta-dark)">${ticketData.ghiChuTuAI || ''}</div></p>
        `);
                    
        $('#chat-header').show();
        $('#chatHeaderName').text(ticketData.tenKhachHang);

        // Xác định Room SignalR chuẩn xác
        const newGroupName = (ticketData.idKhachHang && ticketData.idKhachHang > 0)
        ? `khach_${ticketData.idKhachHang}`
        : `guest_${ticketData.guestSessionId}`;
                    
        if (currentGroupName !== newGroupName) {
        currentGroupName = newGroupName;
        if (hubConnection.state === signalR.HubConnectionState.Connected) {
        await hubConnection.invoke("JoinGroup", currentGroupName);
        }
        }
        $chatInput.prop('disabled', false); $sendButton.prop('disabled', false);
        if (ticketData.trangThai !== 'Đã xử lý') $resolveButton.prop('disabled', false);
        } catch (error) {
        $chatHistory.html('<div class="htnv-empty-state">Lỗi tải dữ liệu.</div>');
        }
        }

        // 4. Cấu hình SignalR Realtime [cite: 33, 34]
        const hubOptions = jwtToken ? { accessTokenFactory: () => jwtToken } : {};
        const hubConnection = new signalR.HubConnectionBuilder()
        .withUrl(apiBaseUrl + "/chatHub", hubOptions)
        .build();
                
        // FIX: Nhận tin nhắn và vẽ trực tiếp (Append) không cần F5
        hubConnection.on("ReceiveMessage", function (message) {
        const idTicket = message.idThongBaoHoTro || message.IdThongBaoHoTro;
        if (currentTicketId && idTicket == currentTicketId) {
        appendSingleMessage(message);
        } else {
        loadTicketList(); // Load lại danh sách bên trái để hiện thông báo mới
        }
        });
            
        hubConnection.on("ReloadTicketList", loadTicketList);
            
        async function startConnection() {
        try { await hubConnection.start(); } catch (err) { console.error("SignalR Error", err); }
        }

        // 5. Sự kiện gửi tin nhắn (Staff Feedback)
        $chatForm.on('submit', async function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        if (!currentTicketId || !currentGroupName || !currentTicketData) return;
                
        const text = $chatInput.val().trim();
        if (!text) return;
                
        $chatInput.val('').prop('disabled', true);
        $sendButton.prop('disabled', true);
 
        try {
        // Ép kiểu số nguyên (int) để khớp với tham số Hub [cite: 13]
        const tId = parseInt(currentTicketId, 10);
        const kId = currentTicketData.idKhachHang ? parseInt(currentTicketData.idKhachHang, 10) : null;
        const gId = currentTicketData.guestSessionId || null;
                
        await hubConnection.invoke("SendMessageFromStaff", currentGroupName, text, tId, kId, gId);
        $('#chatHeaderStatus').text('Đã trả lời');
        } catch (err) {
        alert('Lỗi gửi tin nhắn: ' + err.message);
        } finally {
        $chatInput.prop('disabled', false).focus();
        $sendButton.prop('disabled', false);
        }
        });
            
        // 6. Xử lý đóng phiếu
        $resolveButton.on('click', async function () {
        if (!currentTicketId || !confirm("Đóng phiếu hỗ trợ này?")) return;
        try {
        const res = await fetch(`${apiBaseUrl}/api/web/nhanvien/hotro/resolve/${currentTicketId}`, { method: 'POST', headers: headers });
        if (res.ok) {
        loadTicketList();
        $('#chat-header').hide();
        $chatHistory.html('<div class="htnv-empty-state">Phiếu đã đóng.</div>');
        currentTicketId = null;
        }
        } catch (err) { alert("Lỗi xử lý."); }
        });

        // Tìm kiếm
        $('#ticketSearchInput').on('keyup', function () {
        const term = $(this).val().toLowerCase();
        $('.htnv-ticket-item').each(function () {
        $(this).toggle($(this).text().toLowerCase().includes(term));
        });
        });

        $ticketListContainer.on('click', '.htnv-ticket-item', function () { loadTicketDetail($(this).data('id')); });

        startConnection();
        loadTicketList();
        });
    </script>
}

using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authorization;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.RazorPages;
using Microsoft.Extensions.Configuration;

namespace WebCafebookApi.Pages.Employee
{
    [Authorize]
    public class HoTroKhachHangViewModel : PageModel
    {
        private readonly IConfiguration _configuration;

        public HoTroKhachHangViewModel(IConfiguration configuration)
        {
            _configuration = configuration;
        }

        public string ApiBaseUrl { get; set; } = "";
        public string? JwtToken { get; set; }

        public void OnGet()
        {
            string? url = _configuration.GetSection("ApiSettings")["BaseUrl"];
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(url)) url = _configuration["ApiBaseUrl"];

            ApiBaseUrl = string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(url) ? "http://localhost:5202" : url.TrimEnd('/');
            JwtToken = HttpContext.Session.GetString("JwtToken");
        }
    }
}

    <link rel="stylesheet" href="~/css/PhanHoiKhachHang.css" asp-append-version="true" />

<div class="phkh-container">

                        <span class="material-symbols-outlined align-middle me-1">star</span> Đánh Giá Sản Phẩm

                <li class="nav-item">
                    <button class="nav-link fw-bold" id="feedback-tab" data-bs-toggle="tab" data-bs-target="#feedbacks" type="button">
                        <span class="material-symbols-outlined align-middle me-1">chat</span> Góp Ý Hệ Thống
                    </button>
                </li>
            </ul>
        </div>
        
        <div class="card-body p-4 bg-light">
            <div class="tab-content">
                <div class="tab-pane fade show active" id="reviews">
                    <div id="review-list" class="row g-4">
                    </div>
                </div>

                <div class="tab-pane fade" id="feedbacks">
                    <ul class="nav nav-pills mb-3" id="pills-feedback" role="tablist">
                        <li class="nav-item" role="presentation">
                            <button class="nav-link active rounded-pill px-4 fw-bold" data-bs-toggle="pill" data-bs-target="#pills-pending">Chờ xử lý</button>
                        </li>
                        <li class="nav-item" role="presentation">

                                    <tbody id="feedback-history-body"></tbody>
                                </table>

                <div class="modal fade" id="feedbackEmailModal" tabindex="-1">

                                    <div class="small text-muted" id="fb-customer-info">Gửi tới: ...</div>

                                    "Nội dung khách góp ý..."

                                </div>

                                    <span class="material-symbols-outlined">send</span> XÁC NHẬN GỬI & ĐÓNG GÓP Ý

        <div class="modal-content rounded-4 border-0 shadow">
            <div class="modal-header border-0 pb-0">
                <h5 class="fw-bold">Phản hồi khách hàng</h5>
                <button type="button" class="btn-close" data-bs-dismiss="modal"></button>

                <textarea id="replyText" class="form-control phkh-textarea" rows="4" placeholder="Nhập nội dung phản hồi..."></textarea>
                <button id="btnConfirmReply" class="btn btn-primary w-100 mt-3 fw-bold rounded-pill py-2">GỬI PHẢN HỒI</button>

@section Scripts {
    <script>
        const _apiBaseUrl = "@Model.ApiBaseUrl";
        const _jwtToken = "@Model.JwtToken";
        let _currentReviewId = null;
        let _currentFeedbackId = null;

        async function loadReviews() {
            const res = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/reviews`, { headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` } });
            const data = await res.json();
            const $list = $("#review-list").empty();

            data.forEach(d => {
                let stars = '';
                for(let i=1; i<=5; i++) stars += `<span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-5 ${i <= d.soSao ? 'text-warning' : 'text-light'}">star</span>`;
                
                let repliesHtml = d.danhSachPhanHoi.map(p => `
                    <div class="phkh-reply-item mt-2 p-2 rounded bg-light border-start border-primary border-4">
                        <div class="fw-bold small text-primary">${p.tenNhanVien} <span class="text-muted fw-normal float-end">${new Date(p.ngayTao).toLocaleString()}</span></div>
                        <div class="small">${p.noiDung}</div>
                    </div>
                `).join('');

                $list.append(`
                    <div class="col-md-6 col-xl-4">
                        <div class="card phkh-review-card h-100 border-0 shadow-sm rounded-4 overflow-hidden">
                            <div class="card-body p-4">
                                <div class="d-flex justify-content-between mb-2">
                                    <h6 class="fw-bold text-dark m-0">${d.tenKhachHang}</h6>
                                    <div class="phkh-stars">${stars}</div>
                                </div>
                                <div class="badge bg-info-subtle text-info mb-2">${d.tenSanPham}</div>
                                <p class="text-muted small mb-3">${d.binhLuan || '<i>Không có bình luận</i>'}</p>
                                ${d.hinhAnhUrl ? `<img src="${d.hinhAnhUrl}" class="phkh-review-img mb-3 rounded-3" onerror="this.style.display='none'">` : ''}
                                <div class="phkh-replies-area mb-3">${repliesHtml}</div>
                                <div class="d-flex gap-2">
                                    <button class="btn btn-outline-primary btn-sm flex-grow-1 rounded-pill" onclick="openReplyModal(${d.idDanhGia})">Phản hồi</button>
                                    <button class="btn ${d.trangThai === 'Hiển thị' ? 'btn-outline-danger' : 'btn-outline-success'} btn-sm rounded-pill" onclick="toggleReview(${d.idDanhGia})">
                                        ${d.trangThai === 'Hiển thị' ? 'Ẩn' : 'Hiện'}
                                    </button>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                `);
            });
        }

        async function loadFeedbacks() {
            const res = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/feedbacks`, { headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` } });
            const data = await res.json();
            
            const $pendingBody = $("#feedback-pending-body").empty();
            const $historyBody = $("#feedback-history-body").empty();

            let pendingCount = 0;
            let historyCount = 0;

            data.forEach(g => {
                const dateStr = new Date(g.ngayTao).toLocaleString('vi-VN', {hour: '2-digit', minute:'2-digit', day:'2-digit', month:'2-digit', year:'numeric'});
                
                if (g.trangThai === 'Chờ xử lý') {
                    pendingCount++;
                    // Mã hóa object để quăng vào button
                    const safeGopY = encodeURIComponent(JSON.stringify(g));
                    $pendingBody.append(`
                        <tr>
                            <td class="ps-4"><div class="fw-bold text-dark">${g.hoTen}</div><div class="small text-muted">${g.email}</div></td>
                            <td><div class="text-truncate fw-medium" style="max-width: 350px;">${g.noiDung}</div></td>
                            <td><div class="small text-muted"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-6 align-middle">schedule</span> ${dateStr}</div></td>
                            <td class="text-center pe-4">
                                <button class="btn btn-primary btn-sm rounded-pill px-3 fw-bold shadow-sm" onclick="openFeedbackEmailModal('${safeGopY}')">Xử lý ngay</button>
                            </td>
                        </tr>
                    `);
                } else {
                    historyCount++;
                    $historyBody.append(`
                        <tr>
                            <td class="ps-4"><div class="fw-bold text-dark">${g.hoTen}</div><div class="small text-muted">${g.email}</div></td>
                            <td><div class="text-truncate text-muted" style="max-width: 350px;">${g.noiDung}</div></td>
                            <td><div class="small text-muted">${dateStr}</div></td>
                            <td class="text-center pe-4"><span class="badge bg-success-subtle text-success border border-success-subtle px-3 py-1 rounded-pill"><span class="material-symbols-outlined fs-6 align-middle">done_all</span> ${g.trangThai}</span></td>
                        </tr>
                    `);
                }
            });

            if(pendingCount === 0) $pendingBody.html('<tr><td colspan="4" class="text-center p-5 text-muted fst-italic">Tuyệt vời! Không có góp ý nào đang chờ xử lý.</td></tr>');
            if(historyCount === 0) $historyBody.html('<tr><td colspan="4" class="text-center p-5 text-muted fst-italic">Chưa có lịch sử xử lý.</td></tr>');
        }

        // Functions for Modals & Actions
        function openReplyModal(id) {
            _currentReviewId = id;
            $("#replyText").val('');
            $("#replyModal").modal('show');
        }

        $("#btnConfirmReply").click(async () => {
            const content = $("#replyText").val().trim();
            if(!content) return;
            const res = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/reply-review/${_currentReviewId}`, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` },
                body: JSON.stringify({ noiDung: content })
            });
            if(res.ok) { $("#replyModal").modal('hide'); Swal.fire('Thành công', 'Đã gửi phản hồi', 'success'); loadReviews(); }
        });

        async function toggleReview(id) {
            const res = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/toggle-review/${id}`, { method: 'PUT', headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` } });
            if(res.ok) loadReviews();
        }

        window.openFeedbackEmailModal = function(encodedData) {
            const g = JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(encodedData));
            _currentFeedbackId = g.idGopY;
            $("#fb-customer-info").html(`Gửi tới: <strong class="text-dark">${g.hoTen}</strong> (${g.email})`);
            $("#fb-original-content").text(`"${g.noiDung}"`);
            $("#feedbackEmailText").val('');
            $("#feedbackEmailModal").modal('show');
        };

        $("#btnAutoTemplate").click(function() {
            const template = "Cảm ơn bạn đã đóng góp ý kiến để giúp quán ngày một hoàn thiện hơn. Chúng tôi đã ghi nhận phản hồi của bạn và sẽ khắc phục/cải thiện trong thời gian sớm nhất.\n\nChúc bạn một ngày làm việc tràn đầy năng lượng!";
            $("#feedbackEmailText").val(template);
        });

        $("#btnSendFeedbackEmail").click(async function() {
            const content = $("#feedbackEmailText").val().trim();
            if(!content) return Swal.fire('Lỗi', 'Vui lòng nhập nội dung email', 'warning');

            $("#feedbackEmailModal").modal('hide');
            Swal.fire({
                title: 'Đang gửi Email...',
                html: 'Vui lòng không đóng trình duyệt lúc này.',
                allowOutsideClick: false,
                didOpen: () => { Swal.showLoading(); }
            });

            try {
                const res = await fetch(`${_apiBaseUrl}/reply-feedback/${_currentFeedbackId}`, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Authorization': `Bearer ${_jwtToken}` },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ NoiDungEmail: content })
                });

                if(res.ok) {
                    Swal.fire('Thành công', 'Đã gửi email phản hồi và đóng góp ý!', 'success');
                    loadFeedbacks();
                } else {
                    const err = await res.json();
                    Swal.fire('Lỗi gửi mail', err.message, 'error');
                }
            } catch (error) {
                Swal.fire('Lỗi', 'Mất kết nối máy chủ', 'error');
            }
        });

        // Initialize
        $(document).ready(() => {
            loadReviews();
            loadFeedbacks();
        });
    </script>
}

using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authorization;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.RazorPages;

namespace WebCafebookApi.Pages.Employee
{
    [Authorize]
    public class PhanHoiKhachHangViewModel : PageModel
    {
        private readonly IHttpClientFactory _httpClientFactory;
        public string ApiBaseUrl { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public string? JwtToken { get; set; }

        public PhanHoiKhachHangViewModel(IHttpClientFactory httpClientFactory)
        {
            _httpClientFactory = httpClientFactory;
        }

        public void OnGet()
        {
            JwtToken = HttpContext.Session.GetString("JwtToken");
            var client = _httpClientFactory.CreateClient("ApiClient");
            ApiBaseUrl = $"{client.BaseAddress}api/web/nhanvien/PhanHoiKhachHangWeb";
        }
    }
}
